Vertex shader: ../p6/cut_by_cylinder.vert
-----------------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |in vec3 position;
 13 |in vec3 normal;
 14 |
 15 |
 16 |// Posición de la fuente en el espacio de la cámara
 17 |uniform vec3 lightpos;
 18 |// Color difuso del objeto
 19 |uniform vec4 diffuseColor = vec4(0.8, 0.3, 0.3, 1.0);
 20 |
 21 |out vec4 color;
 22 |
 23 |void main() {
 24 |	// Normal en el espacio de la cámara
 25 |	vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix *normal);
 26 |	// Vértice en el espacio de la cámara
 27 |	vec4 pos4 = vec4(position, 1.0);
 28 |	vec3 eposition=vec3(modelviewMatrix * pos4);
 29 |	// Cálculo de la iluminación
 30 |	color = max(0.0, dot(eN, normalize(lightpos-eposition))) * diffuseColor;
 31 |	//gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * pos4;
 32 |	gl_Position = eposition;
 33 |}

 22 |void main() {
 23 |	// Normal del vértice en el espacio de la cámara
 24 |	vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix *normal);

 28 |	// Cálculo de la iluminación
 29 |	color = max(0.0, dot(eN, normalize(lightpos-eposition.xyz))) * diffuseColor;
 30 |	gl_Position = eposition;
 31 |}

 23 |
 24 |void main() {
 25 |	vec3 cylinderPosNormalized = 
 26 |

 28 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 29 |		if (distance(gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz, cylinderPosNormalized) < 1) {
 30 |			count += 1;
 31 |		}
 32 |	}
 33 |
 34 |	if (count < 3) {
 35 |		for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {

[Sun May  1 17:06:35 2022] ERR: [program.cpp (223)] Error compilando el shader:0(36) : error C7623: implicit narrowing of type from "vec3" to "float"

Geometry shader: ../p6/cut_by_cylinder.geom
-------------------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |layout (triangles) in;
 13 |layout (triangle_strip, max_vertices = 3) out;
 14 |
 15 |// Cylinder
 16 |uniform float cylinderRadius; // radio del cilindro
 17 |uniform float cylinderHeight; // altura del cilindro
 18 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // dirección del eje (vector unitario)
 19 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // centro de la base del cilindro
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];
 22 |out vec4 fragColor;
 23 |
 24 |void main() {
 25 |	int count = 0;
 26 |	vec3 cylinderPosA = vec3(vec4(cylinderPos, 1)*modelviewMatrix);
 27 |	vec3 cylinderPosB = cylinderPos + cylinderAxis*cylinderHeight;
 28 |	cylinderPosB = vec3(vec4(cylinderPosB, 1)*modelviewMatrix);
 29 |
 30 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 31 |		float check_cylinderA = dot(gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz - cylinderPosA, 
 32 |			cylinderPosB - cylinderPosA);
 33 |		float check_cylinderB = dot(gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz - cylinderPosB, 
 34 |			cylinderPosB - cylinderPosA);
 35 |		float check_cylinderR = abs(cross(gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz - cylinderPosA, 
 36 |			cylinderPosB - cylinderPosA)) /abs(cylinderPosB - cylinderPosA);
 37 |		if (check_cylinderA >= 0 && check_cylinderB <= 0 
 38 |			&& check_cylinderR < cylinderRadius) {
 39 |			count += 1;
 40 |		}
 41 |	}
 42 |
 43 |	if (count < 3) {
 44 |		for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 45 |			gl_Position = projMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 46 |			if (count == 1) {
 47 |				fragColor = vec4(0, 1, 0, 1);
 48 |			}
 49 |			else if (count == 2) {
 50 |				fragColor = vec4(1, 0, 0, 1);
 51 |			}
 52 |			else {
 53 |				fragColor = color[i];
 54 |			}
 55 |			EmitVertex();
 56 |		}
 57 |		EndPrimitive();
 58 |	}
 59 |}

Geometry shader: ../p6/cut_by_cylinder.geom
-------------------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |
 12 |layout (triangles) in;
 13 |layout (triangle_strip, max_vertices = 3) out;
 14 |
 15 |// Cylinder
 16 |uniform float cylinderRadius; // radio del cilindro
 17 |uniform float cylinderHeight; // altura del cilindro
 18 |uniform vec3 cylinderAxis; // dirección del eje (vector unitario)
 19 |uniform vec3 cylinderPos; // centro de la base del cilindro
 20 |
 21 |in vec4 color[3];
 22 |out vec4 fragColor;
 23 |
 24 |void main() {
 25 |	int count = 0;
 26 |	vec3 cylinderPosA = vec3(modelviewMatrix*vec4(cylinderPos, 1));
 27 |	vec3 cylinderPosB = cylinderPos + cylinderAxis*cylinderHeight;
 28 |	cylinderPosB = vec3(*modelviewMatrix*vec4(cylinderPosB, 1));
 29 |
 30 |	for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 31 |		float check_cylinderA = dot(gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz - cylinderPosA, 
 32 |			cylinderPosB - cylinderPosA);
 33 |		float check_cylinderB = dot(gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz - cylinderPosB, 
 34 |			cylinderPosB - cylinderPosA);
 35 |		float check_cylinderR = length(cross(gl_in[i].gl_Position.xyz - cylinderPosA, 
 36 |			cylinderPosB - cylinderPosA)) /length(cylinderPosB - cylinderPosA);
 37 |		if (check_cylinderA >= 0 && check_cylinderB <= 0 
 38 |			&& check_cylinderR < cylinderRadius) {
 39 |			count += 1;
 40 |		}
 41 |	}
 42 |
 43 |	if (count < 3) {
 44 |		for (int i = 0; i < gl_in.length(); i++) {
 45 |			gl_Position = projMatrix * gl_in[i].gl_Position;
 46 |			if (count == 1) {
 47 |				fragColor = vec4(0, 1, 0, 1);
 48 |			}
 49 |			else if (count == 2) {
 50 |				fragColor = vec4(1, 0, 0, 1);
 51 |			}
 52 |			else {
 53 |				fragColor = color[i];
 54 |			}
 55 |			EmitVertex();
 56 |		}
 57 |		EndPrimitive();
 58 |	}
 59 |}
